        checks = []
        if conditions.get("title", {}).get("contains"):
            checks.append(self._contains_any(issue.name, conditions["title"]["contains"]))
        if conditions.get("body", {}).get("contains"):
            body = issue.description_stripped or strip_tags(issue.description_html or "")
            checks.append(self._contains_any(body, conditions["body"]["contains"]))
        if conditions.get("project"):
            checks.append(self._project_matches(issue.project, conditions["project"]))
        if not checks:
            return False
        if conditions["match"] == TriageAutomationRule.MatchMode.ANY.value:
            return any(checks)
        return all(checks)

    @staticmethod
    def _contains_any(value, needles):
        haystack = (value or "").casefold()
        return any(str(needle).casefold() in haystack for needle in needles)

    @staticmethod
    def _project_matches(project, condition):
        checks = []
        if condition.get("ids"):
            checks.append(str(project.id) in {str(project_id) for project_id in condition["ids"]})
        if condition.get("identifiers"):
            checks.append(project.identifier.upper() in {identifier.upper() for identifier in condition["identifiers"]})
        if condition.get("names"):
            checks.append(project.name in set(condition["names"]))
        return any(checks)

    @staticmethod
    def _apply_priority(issue, rule, actions, applied_actions, conflicts, no_change):
        priority = actions.get("priority")
        if not priority:
            return

        current = issue.priority or "none"
        if current == priority:
            no_change["priority"] = priority
            return

        if current != "none" and rule.conflict_behavior == TriageAutomationRule.ConflictBehavior.PRESERVE:
            conflicts.append(
                {
                    "field": "priority",
                    "reason": "existing_value_preserved",
                    "current": current,
                    "requested": priority,
                    "rule_id": str(rule.id),
                }
            )
            return

        issue.priority = priority
        issue.save(update_fields=["priority", "updated_at"])
        applied_actions["priority"] = {"old": current, "new": priority}

    @staticmethod
    def _apply_labels(issue, rule, actions, applied_actions, conflicts, no_change):
        requested = set(actions.get("label_ids", []))
        if not requested:
            return

        live = set(
            str(label_id)
            for label_id in Label.objects.filter(project=issue.project, id__in=requested).values_list("id", flat=True)
        )
        stale = sorted(requested - live)
        if stale:
            conflicts.append(
                {
                    "field": "labels",
                    "reason": "label_not_in_project",
                    "label_ids": stale,
                    "rule_id": str(rule.id),
                }
            )

        existing = set(
            str(label_id) for label_id in IssueLabel.objects.filter(issue=issue).values_list("label_id", flat=True)
        )
        to_add = sorted(live - existing)
        if not to_add:
            no_change["label_ids"] = sorted(live)
            return

        actor_id = issue.created_by_id
        IssueLabel.objects.bulk_create(
            [
                IssueLabel(
                    issue=issue,
                    label_id=label_id,
                    project_id=issue.project_id,
                    workspace_id=issue.workspace_id,
                    created_by_id=actor_id,
                    updated_by_id=actor_id,
                )
                for label_id in to_add
            ],
            batch_size=10,
            ignore_conflicts=True,
        )
        applied_actions["label_ids"] = to_add

    def _apply_assignees(self, issue, rule, actions, applied_actions, conflicts, no_change):
        requested = set(actions.get("assignee_ids", []))
        if not requested:
            return

        live = set(
            str(member_id)
            for member_id in ProjectMember.objects.filter(
                project=issue.project,
                member_id__in=requested,
                role__gte=15,
                is_active=True,
            ).values_list("member_id", flat=True)
        )
        stale = sorted(requested - live)
        if stale:
            conflicts.append(
                {
                    "field": "assignees",
                    "reason": "assignee_not_active_project_member",
                    "assignee_ids": stale,
                    "rule_id": str(rule.id),
                }
            )

        existing = set(
            str(assignee_id)
            for assignee_id in IssueAssignee.objects.filter(issue=issue).values_list("assignee_id", flat=True)
        )
        to_add = sorted(live - existing)
        if not to_add:
            no_change["assignee_ids"] = sorted(live)
            return

        actor_id = self.actor_id or issue.created_by_id
        IssueAssignee.objects.bulk_create(
            [
                IssueAssignee(
                    issue=issue,
                    assignee_id=assignee_id,
                    project_id=issue.project_id,
                    workspace_id=issue.workspace_id,
                    created_by_id=actor_id,
                    updated_by_id=actor_id,
                )
                for assignee_id in to_add
            ],
            batch_size=10,
            ignore_conflicts=True,
        )
        applied_actions["assignee_ids"] = to_add

    @staticmethod
    def _status_for(applied_actions, conflicts):
        if conflicts:
            return TriageAutomationRun.Status.CONFLICT
        if applied_actions:
            return TriageAutomationRun.Status.APPLIED
        return TriageAutomationRun.Status.NO_CHANGE

    @staticmethod
    def _snapshot(issue):
        return {
            "priority": issue.priority,
            "label_ids": sorted(
                str(label_id) for label_id in IssueLabel.objects.filter(issue=issue).values_list("label_id", flat=True)
            ),
            "assignee_ids": sorted(
                str(assignee_id)
                for assignee_id in IssueAssignee.objects.filter(issue=issue).values_list("assignee_id", flat=True)
            ),
        }

    def _create_issue_activity(self, issue, rule, before, after):
        actor_id = self.actor_id or issue.created_by_id
        IssueActivity.objects.create(
            issue=issue,
            actor_id=actor_id,
            verb="updated",
            field="triage_automation",
            old_value=_json_dump(before),
            new_value=_json_dump(after),
            comment=f'Plane triage automation applied "{rule.name}"',
            project_id=issue.project_id,
            workspace_id=issue.workspace_id,
            epoch=int(timezone.now().timestamp()),
            created_by_id=actor_id,
            updated_by_id=actor_id,
        )

    def _create_failed_run(self, rule, exc):
        issue = Issue.all_objects.filter(pk=self.issue_id).first()
        return TriageAutomationRun.objects.create(
            rule=rule,
            issue=issue,
            project_id=rule.project_id,
            workspace_id=rule.workspace_id,
            trigger=self.trigger,
            status=TriageAutomationRun.Status.FAILED,
            matched=False,
            conditions_snapshot=rule.conditions,
            actions_snapshot=rule.actions,
            error=str(exc)[:2000],
            correlation_id=self.correlation_id,
        )


def run_triage_automation_rules(issue_id, actor_id=None, trigger="manual"):
    return TriageAutomationExecutor(issue_id=issue_id, actor_id=actor_id, trigger=trigger).run()
```

</details>

class ProjectBaseModel(BaseModel):
    project = models.ForeignKey(Project, on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name="project_%(class)s")
    workspace = models.ForeignKey("db.Workspace", on_delete=models.CASCADE, related_name="workspace_%(class)s")

    class Meta:
        abstract = True

    def save(self, *args, **kwargs):
        self.workspace = self.project.workspace
        super(ProjectBaseModel, self).save(*args, **kwargs)

def validate_review_file(path: Path, review: dict[str, Any], workspace: Path) -> list[str]:
    blockers = []
    required = ("artifact_contract_version", "review_id", "tier", "severity", "finding", "artifact", "evidence", "recommendation", "blocking")
    for field in required:
        if field not in review:
            blockers.append(f"{path.relative_to(workspace)} missing {field}")
    if review.get("artifact_contract_version") != CONTRACT_VERSION:
        blockers.append(f"{path.relative_to(workspace)} artifact_contract_version mismatch")
    if review.get("severity") not in {"critical", "major", "minor", "note"}:
        blockers.append(f"{path.relative_to(workspace)} invalid severity")
    if not isinstance(review.get("blocking"), bool):
        blockers.append(f"{path.relative_to(workspace)} blocking must be boolean")
    if review.get("severity") == "critical" and review.get("blocking") is not True:
        blockers.append(f"{path.relative_to(workspace)} critical severity must be blocking")
    return blockers


def validate_verification_if_started(workspace: Path, state: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:
    gate = (state.get("gates") or {}).get("verification")
    if gate not in {"drafted", "approved", "delegated", "complete"}:
        return []
    blockers = []
    verification_review = workspace / "reviews/verification-review.md"
    if not verification_review.exists():
        blockers.append("verification gate requires reviews/verification-review.md")
    final_output = workspace / "evidence/final-verification-output.log"
    if not final_output.exists():
        blockers.append("verification gate requires evidence/final-verification-output.log")
    blockers.extend(validate_review_minimum(workspace))
    return blockers


def validate_finish_if_started(workspace: Path, state: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:
    gate = (state.get("gates") or {}).get("finish")
    if gate not in {"drafted", "approved", "delegated", "complete"} and state.get("current_step") not in {"finish", "promote"}:
        return []
    blockers = []
    if not (workspace / "feature-card.md").exists():
        blockers.append("finish requires feature-card.md")
    stale = state.get("stale") or {}
    if stale.get("feature_card"):
        blockers.append("finish blocked by stale feature_card")
    if stale.get("canonical_docs"):
        blockers.append("finish blocked by stale canonical_docs")
    if (state.get("gates") or {}).get("verification") != "complete":
        blockers.append("finish requires verification gate complete")
    blockers.extend(validate_all_slices_complete(workspace))
    blockers.extend(validate_evidence_minimum(workspace))
```
